2/26/24, 20:14 - Wafa: 1. Create Advance Computer Vision Tech :
Developing advanced computer vision algorithms to enhance real-time object recognition
and analysis for diverse applications.
Link for reference: https://www.theclickreader.com/open-source-computer-vision-projects-with-tutorials/

2. Open Source AI for Social Good:
Develop an open-source AI solution that addresses a social or environmental challenge.
This could include projects related to healthcare, education, climate change, or any other
area where AI can make a positive impact.
Link for reference: https://github.com/neeleshsaxena/Tele-HealthCare

3. AR/VR Accessibility Toolkit:
Create an open-source toolkit that enhances accessibility in AR/VR applications. The
toolkit should include features like voice navigation, gesture recognition, and other
accessibility enhancements to make AR/VR experiences more inclusive.
Link for reference: https://github.com/A11YTK/A11YTK

4. Algorithmic Fairness Dashboard:
Build an open-source dashboard for assessing and visualizing the fairness of algorithms.
The dashboard should provide insights into the potential biases in AI models and assist
developers in making their algorithms more fair and ethical.
Link for reference: https://github.com/synthesized-io/fairlens

5. Open Source Web Security Scanner:
Develop an open-source web security scanner tool that helps developers identify and
mitigate security vulnerabilities in web applications. The tool should support automated
scanning, report generation, and integration with popular web development frameworks.
Link for reference: https://github.com/infosecsecurity/Spaghetti

6. AI-powered Code Review Assistant:
Create an AI-powered open-source tool that assists developers in code reviews. The tool
should analyze code changes, identify potential issues, and provide suggestions for
improvement, helping maintain code quality and consistency.
Link for reference: https://github.com/joelybahh/code-buddy

7. AR/VR Education Platform:
Build an open-source AR/VR platform for educational purposes. The platform should
allow educators to create immersive learning experiences for various subjects, promoting
interactive and engaging learning environments.
Link for reference: https://externlabs.com/blogs/open-source-platform-for-ar-and-vr/

8. Open Source Personal Health Assistant:
Develop an open-source personal health assistant that leverages AI to provide
health-related information, reminders for medications, and suggestions for maintaining a
healthy lifestyle. The system should prioritize user privacy and data security.
Link for reference: https://github.com/topics/personal-health-record

9. Algorithm Visualization Library:
Create an open-source library for visualizing algorithms. The library should support a
wide range of algorithms, providing interactive visualizations that help users understand
the inner workings of algorithms and data structures.
Link for reference: https://github.com/topics/algorithm-visualization

10. Web Accessibility Checker:
Build an open-source tool that automatically checks web applications for accessibility
compliance. The tool should identify and provide suggestions to fix accessibility issues,
ensuring that web content is accessible to users with disabilities.
Link for reference: https://github.com/topics/accessibility-checker

11. Cross-Platform Mobile App Framework:
Develop an open-source framework for building cross-platform mobile applications. The
framework should support seamless development for both Android and iOS platforms,
offering a unified codebase for efficient app development.
Link for reference: https://github.com/topics/cross-platform-app
